20/04/20, 11:57 am - Atul Shelar: Please pass on the below mentioned opportunity to COEP Comp/IT students in third and final year.

We are working on a business idea to disrupt Indian education system.
It's an early-stage startup in the EdTech space, founded by COEP, IIM, IIT alums with ample amount of Consulting, Product Management, Startup experience among others.

Location: Work from home

The Idea: Disrupt education system in India by revolutionizing all touch points in a Student's life.

The portfolio of services under this umbrella are as follows:
- Acharya Academy: Digitizing K12 education in Tier 2 and Tier 3 cities. Connecting quality teachers in Tier 1 cities with students in Tier 2/3 cities
- aksh - aage kya socha hai? A Career Counselling Platform: Detailed psychometric analysis and glimpses into a day of all kind of professionals to help students make informed career choice
- Metamorph - An all-round development center: All-in-one hobby center to try out and pursue various extra curricular activities and a platform to teach life-skills to students
- EddyTech: Technology Solution to empower all the offerings

While various people may have talked about it in various forms, we are actually translating the thought into action!
Three of us
- Sumit Singare (COEP'14, IIMA'18)
- Anirudha Seksaria (IIT Delhi'13, IIMA'17)
- Dnyaneshwar Mutkule (COEP'15), have started working on this idea since last few months and we have started getting a good traction in Tier 2 and Tier 3 cities.

As we build this solution, we are also looking to hire bright & energetic folks in our Tech team in Part-time/Full-time capacity.

Who should be looking to join: Those who
- aren't afraid of uncertainty and find their way through chaos and ambiguity.
- aren't afraid of falling but learn how to do better the next time
- like to build from scratch and not to copy
- value learning and growth at par with money
- Hands on knowledge of Java, Python, DBMS, SQL
- If you are third year B.Tech student looking for an internship
- If you are final year B.Tech/M.Tech student looking for a full time job
- Knowledge of React/Angular JS is a plus

CGPA No Bar

Who should specifically not join: Those who
- expect structure and well-defined processes right from the start
- need to have clearly defined problems and roles
- are happy offering advice but would ideally not want to implement

Compensation: At par with industry standards

If you are interested, please send your resumes on
